Title: Succubus Queen, Fallen Saintess, Vampire Princess—they're all mine! This profession is outrageous!

The classroom at Jungqings third academy for professionals buzzed with excitement. A lively chatter hung in the air one week after the awakening ceremony. The students had just completed their beginner missions and were fervently exchanging their tips and tricks for leveling up. My shield warrior is absolutely unstoppable. I've got a passive 10% melee damage reflection. Leveling up is a breeze. A burly male student boasted loudly. Someone next to him immediately poured cold water on his enthusiasm. Damage reflection only works in melee. What are you going to do if you face a ranged monster? You'd be toast. That's why I need a team. Duh. Not everyone can pull off being a lone wolf like you. Amid the noisy crowd, Guuan was the odd one out. He sat alone by the window, disengaged from the conversation around him, quietly organizing his books with his head down. Suddenly, a folded piece of paper slipped out of his notebook and fluttered to the ground. Guuan bent down to pick it up and unfolded it, revealing a neat line of handwriting. Meet me on the rooftop after class. A small heart was doodled next to the message, but there was no signature. Seriously, people still write notes like this? Isn't texting way easier? Guu Yuan muttered to himself, shaking his head in mild disbelief. He crumpled the note into a ball and tossed it aside. Before his professional awakening, he might have entertained a fleeting thought that a girl could be secretly in love with him. But now, to him, any sort of confession felt more like a practical joke than a genuine sentiment. Guu Yuan wasn't just any student. He was a transmigrator, someone who had crossed over from another world. For 18 years, he had lived in this place, a world vastly different from his original home, Blue Planet. Here, the rules of reality intertwined with those of a game. A thousand years ago, the game system descended upon this world, unleashing monsters across the land. At the same time, humans awakened bizarre and extraordinary powers known as professions. From staff wielding mages and battleh hardened warriors to chefs cooking culinary masterpieces and farmers tending to crops, everyone had found their role within the new system. Combat professionals took to the front lines to fend off the monstrous threats, protecting humanity, while non-combat professionals supported society from the rear, working to ensure the world functioned smoothly. Although authorities constantly preached that no profession was inherently superior to another, everyone understood the harsh truth. True freedom and influence only belonged to those who rose to become mighty combat professionals, the protagonists of this world. Fortunately for Guuan, he had awakened as well. His profession, a rare and unique hidden class, abyss walker. He was the only one in existence with this profession, allowing him to form packs with demons and fallen angels from the abyss, summoning them to fight by his side. It sounded unimaginably powerful. But as with all things that attracted envy, the price was equally harrowing. To forge a pact with a demon, one had to offer their own soul and flesh. It was undeniably an evil profession. The school principal hadn't minced words in warning him. If Guu Yuan insisted on associating with demons, he would ultimately lose himself. Torn apart by the whispers of corrupted angels and the seductive torment of succubi queens. Even his home room teacher had implored him to give up on this doomed path, claiming even working in a factory would be better than heading down a road with no return. Guuan had nodded and agreed outwardly, but kept one critical truth to himself, the soul and flesh required for sacrifices didn't necessarily have to be his own. Others could work just fine. On his profession status panel, the methods for packs were listed clearly. Sacrifice 10 living goblins to summon a minor demon. Sacrifice 10 living wasteland wolves to summon a hellhound. Monsters were humanity's natural enemies, the target of every professional hunt, using them as sacrificial offerings. Guu Yuan didn't feel an ounce of guilt about it. But this approach could only bind him to low-level disposable minions with no potential for growth. To summon those famous and formidable elite units, the ones with names and unmatched potential, required rarer, higher quality sacrifices, for example, human professionals. Sacrifice one living professional to summon Succubus Queen Yaerna. The moment Guan saw this entry, he truly comprehended the dark terror of the Abyss Walker class. It wasn't a test of his resistance to corruption or moral compromise, but rather a raw, unfiltered challenge to his humanity and human nature. It was the one thing most susceptible to temptation. Guuan's gaze instinctively roamed across the classroom, pausing momentarily on one student after another. Everyone here was a newly awakened professional, still inexperienced and relatively weak. It would be easy to choose someone as his target, a so-called lucky one. The thought crossed his mind more than once, yet each time he squashed it with sheer willpower, sacrificing an innocent classmate for his ambition. No, he couldn't go that far. Not yet. Of course, this world wasn't devoid of scumbags. Many corrupt and vile professionals deserve to be eliminated. Guu Yuan wouldn't hesitate to sacrifice such individuals. But the problem was with his current strength, tracking down and taking on those people was a death sentence. He wasn't strong enough to survive. "Tomorrow's the newbie trial," Guu Yuan thought to himself. "Looks like I'll have to rely on my few minor demons." The newbie trial was every professional's first significant turning point, a one-time opportunity in their entire life. Top guilds used this trial to evaluate a students potential, determining whether to offer them a chance to join. Securing a place in a prestigious guild guaranteed exponentially faster growth 10, even 100 times faster than joining a lesser guild. Only by standing out in this trial could Guuan hope to gather the strength necessary to hunt down villains and summon truly powerful demon leaders without betraying his conscience. While he had promised his home room teacher that he would abandon his professional ambitions and opt for a quiet life as a factory worker, Guuan had secretly spent the past week leveling up, reaching level five and qualifying for the trial. The problem? His minor demons weren't nearly strong enough to earn him an S-rank rating, the standard top tier guilds demanded. At this point, should I summon the succubus queen before the trial? There's no chance, but that doesn't mean I can sacrifice my principles," Guuan said, shaking his head and retracting the dangerous glint in his eyes. "If passing the trial meant killing innocent people, then how is that any different from becoming corrupted by the abyss?" At that moment, a strong, almost overwhelming perfume wafted over. "Guian looked up to see Shinlen, the school's notorious beauty, standing next to his desk." Ku Yuan," she began in an unnaturally sugary voice, overly sweet and disingenuous as her smile. "I've liked you for a long time. Will you be my boyfriend?" She thrust a bouquet of roses toward him dramatically. The previously noisy classroom fell into an immediate hush. All eyes turned to Guu Yuan as if spotlights were suddenly beaming down on him. For three long seconds, the silence lingered before snickers erupted from the back row. Guu Yuan tilted his head slightly, glancing past Shinlens overly performative grin to look at the classrooms rear. There sat Joo, Shinlians actual boyfriend, casually lounging with his lackey. Humor danced in their eyes as they watched the scene unfold like spectators at an amateur play. In an instant, Guu Yuan understood everything. They were playing truth or dare, and he was just the punchline for their twisted little game. Guu Yuans gaze returned to Shunlen, lingering only briefly. She was undeniably beautiful, worthy of her reputation as the school flower, but her beauty only stirred a sense of disgust deep within him. For a few beats, he said nothing. Then, without a word, he reached out and took the roses. "Wo!" A collective gasp rippled through the room, followed by uncontrollable laughter erupting in the back row. He actually believed it. one cried out between fits of laughter. He seriously bought it. Oh my god, I can't breathe. You're a genius for this one. And Shenlen, such a kind soul, coming down from her pedestal to comfort our fallen prodigy. The mockery filled the classroom, but the mirth faded somewhat as Shenlans face froze in mortification. She turned and glared at the back row. Are you satisfied now? She hissed under her breath, her tone barely masking her irritation. Then half-heartedly, she shifted back to Guu Yuan, trying to salvage the situation. Um, Guu Yuan, she started, attempting to explain. You might have misunderstood. We were just playing. Her words died on her lips. The roses in Guu Yuan's hand were withering before her very eyes. The vibrant red petals dulled to a lifeless gray as they shriveled up. the once lush green stems turning yellow and brittle. It was as though every ounce of vitality had been sucked out in mere seconds. It was Guu Yuan's abyssal ability, a power of corruption that consumed whatever it touched. In a handful of heartbeats, the delicate bouquet became nothing more than a rotting husk. Shenmlans face twisted, her demeanor shifting from cheerful to offended in a heartbeat. What is the meaning of this, Guuan? She snapped, her tone icy. Gu Yuan didn't flinch. Releasing his fingers, he let the remnants of the dried roses crumble and scatter onto the floor. I accepted your flowers out of basic respect for you as a woman. I discarded them to respect myself. For the second time that day, the room fell utterly silent. Shenlan's face flushed an alarming shade of crimson. This time not from suave charm, but a mix of shame and fury. Across the room, a few students who had initially been entertained now bore expressions of subtle awe and respect. "Man, Guu Yuan still has that cool factor," someone murmured. "Yeah, no wonder he used to be number one. Even now, after everything, he's got guts. I'll admit that felt so satisfying to watch. Joe's crew took it way too far." Exactly. Honestly, if it weren't for some bad luck, Guuan would have never fallen to their level. They wouldn't even dare mess with him otherwise. The murmurs seemed to hit Jo like slaps to the face. Red-faced and humiliated at the failure of his prank, he slammed his hand on his desk and bolted to his feet. "Guian," he roared, his voice shaking with rage. "You're asking for it, huh?" Pointing aggressively at Guu Yuan, he began yelling a string of obscenities. You awakened that messed up ability. So what? It doesn't make you special. And now you think you can act all high and mighty. Shinlen, regaining her composure and venom, crossed her arms and sneered. Seriously, some people should be grateful they're even acknowledged. Instead, they bite the hand that feeds them. I was just being nice, but clearly that was a mistake. Her lackey chimed in unison like a bad choir. Yeah, Shinlen practically did him a favor. Quick, someone record this. Might be the last time a girl talks to him. Not even a miracle could help that guy now. That face of his. Best use it to earn a few bucks on, you know, those websites. Guu Yuan couldn't help but chuckle softly. The sound wasn't loud, but its edge was sharp enough to slice through the rising tension. The casual laugh only triggered Joobo further, pushing him over the edge. You think this is funny, huh? Joe grabbed a chair, brandishing it like a weapon. Come on, then. Let's settle this oneonone. Joe Bo, what are you doing? Put that down. Several male students jumped up to intervene. A girl shook her head with disdain. Jo, are you serious right now? Guianuan's ability might have side effects, but at the end of the day, it's still a combat class. He's no pushover, she said, her glare sharp as daggers. Exactly. And guess what? His pre-awwakening stats were maxed out. You think you can take on someone who started with full attributes? We're not talking about some regular Joe here. The sharp reminder seemed to hit Joe like a bucket of cold water. Hesitation flickered across his face. Pre-awwakening attributes referred to a person's natural abilities before they even awakened to a class. Guuan incredibly had hit the cap in strength, agility, endurance, and mental resilience before his awakening, something rarely achieved. Even inactive or untrained, Guuan's total combat potential wasn't something to scoff at. More importantly, Guu Yuan wasn't helpless. His abyssal ability was destructive, and there was no telling how far he'd be willing to go if pushed. No one wanted to test what would happen if he turned that power on a person instead of a flower. Wang Hu, you're up. Did he become a berserker? drag him out and teach him a hard lesson. Wang Hu, who was called out, hesitated for a moment, a trace of unease flashing across his face. Berserker was just a standard class, not even rare by any means. On the other hand, Guu Yuan had a hidden class and was gifted with maxed initial stats. First of all, vampire hunter refers to a type of combat professional. This is not an official profession, but rather an ancient trade. During the chaotic era before the establishment of the human federation, vampires from other realms had infiltrated human society on a large scale. Many human professionals eager for immortality or power. On the path to seeking power, there were always some humans who chose shortcuts, actively requesting transformation by vampires, becoming the first batch of halfhuman, half- ghost blood servants. However, the human heart is unpredictable. Among these individuals, some can still adhere to their principles, drinking only animal blood. Others have completely succumbed to their desires, taking pleasure in hunting their former compatriots and being scornfully referred to as human blood traders. To combat this evil force, a special group known as vampire hunters emerged. Their identities vary. They might be warriors, mages, or even ordinary professionals, but as long as they specialize in eliminating blood traders, they are bestowed with the title of vampire hunter. With the establishment of the new order, those heinous blood traitors have long been eradicated, while law-abiding blood servants have gained legal citizenship and are protected by the law. Without prey, hunters naturally faded away. Nowadays, those who claim to be vampire hunters are mostly profit-driven gold farmers, specializing in exploring secret realms with vampire backgrounds to profit from alchemical materials. Holy light combatants excel at healing, whether for individuals or groups. However, her ability could reverse this healing light into true damage that corrods flesh and blood. Lan Yuding would definitely notice his disappearance and call upon the guild members to guard the place where he vanished. But he never expected that among these guild members there would be such a heavyweight guest. Guuan raised his head and looked at the ice throne floating above. There was only one person in the world who could sit there. The highest peak of the northern territory, the guardian stone of the frost rift, the uncrowned king of Linuan city, the president of the winter guild, bitter cold monarch, Lan Shangong. Just like on television, Lan Shangong had short ice blue hair, ice blue eyes, and even the stubble on his chin was ice blue. At this moment, this top tier powerhouse of the fourth rank was standing at the edge of the ice throne, looking down at him from above. That gaze was not friendly. However, this was also reasonable. Guuan's gaze shifted slightly, and on one side of the ice throne stood a graceful figure. It was Lon Ruatong. She was gazing at him from afar, her eyes slightly red, clearly having just cried. The fact that the Frost King personally descended here was undoubtedly thanks to her efforts. Guuan somewhat understood Lan Shang Dongs feelings at this moment. Being woken up in the middle of the night by his beloved daughter to come and save a complete stranger, a young boy would feel inexplicable to any father. Moreover, this father's status was far beyond that of ordinary people. Under normal circumstances, this lofty frost king probably wouldn't even spare him a glance. But then again, he wasn't just some ordinary young man. He was the one her precious daughter had been longing for. Thinking of this, Guuan straightened his back even more. He politely declined the medical staff's offer for further examination, smiling as he thanked them. Then his gaze swept past the crowd and locked onto the monarch seated on the ice throne. "Junior Guuan, thank you for gracing us with your presence, Frost King." His voice was clear and resolute as he performed a standard chest salute. Under your guidance, I vow to become the winter storm that sweeps through the frost abyss rift. To become the storm that sweeps through the frost abyss, this is the motto of the winter guild. Personally penned by Lon Shangdong. For someone of his level, any flattering words are unnecessary. He doesn't need gratitude from a newcomer, nor does he care about so-called repayment. Guuan only needs to fulfill his duties as a member of the Winter Guild, which is the best way to repay this king and the least likely to go wrong. Sure enough, after these words were spoken, Lan Shan Dongs sharp, icelike gaze noticeably softened. Liang Dong even nodded slightly at Guu Yuan. He took a few steps back and sat steadily back on the ice throne, though his gaze remained fixed on Guuan. He was scrutinizing scrutinizing this young man who had been personally recommended by his son and whose daughter had pleaded with him to intervene. Not bad. After a moment, Liangdong gave his first evaluation. The young man beneath the throne was dignified and composed, showing no signs of panic or fear after narrowly escaping danger. Even when faced with the overwhelming presence of the cityguards, the experts from the winter guild and himself as a top tier powerhouse, the boy merely paused slightly without displaying the slightest hint of cowardice. Such psychological resilience is truly rare in someone only 18 or 19 years old. Of course, beyond his temperament, what Lan Shang Dong admired even more was Guu Yuan strength. In his youth, he had also been trapped in that kind of special secret realm capable of devouring everything. So he knew better than anyone how perilous it was inside. It was not an opportunity, but a trap specifically designed to ensnare and kill combat professionals. Anyone who could walk out of such a place alive undoubtedly possessed extraordinary strength. Very strong. This was Lan Shandong's second evaluation of Guuan. Courageous and powerful. Under normal circumstances, upon encountering such talent, Lan Shang Dong would never just sit idly by. He would surely offer loud praise. But Guu Yuan was different. To him, Guuan was not just a talent, but also a wild wolf threatening his precious daughter. Lan Shang Dong had long noticed that his daughter definitely liked this boy named Guu Yuan. Ever since his daughter grew up, he had never seen her care so much about someone, not even himself, as her father had received such treatment. Thinking of this, Lan Shang Dong felt a pang of sourness in his heart. He had thought that with his daughter's cold and frosty personality, no man would be able to get close to her easily. If she could get married by the age of 27 or 28, it would already be a blessing. But what happened? She had just turned 18 not long ago, and now a wild wolf had appeared at their doorstep. How infuriating. 18 was the prime of youth, the most beautiful time of life, and now she was about to be taken away. Lan Shangdong sat on the throne, his brows furrowing tighter and tighter, even mentally rehearsing the scenes that might unfold next. With the atmosphere as it was, his daughter would probably jump straight off the throne, give that boy a heartfelt hug, and then plat a passionate kiss on him. "No!" The image in his mind shattered Lan Shang Dongs heart. Just as he was immersed in sorrow, Lan Ruatong suddenly spoke up. "Dad, let's go home." Langdong was stunned. Go home. Just go home like that. This doesn't make sense. At this moment, aren't you supposed to leave your old father behind and jump down to give your little boyfriend a hug? That's how it always plays out on TV. Liang Dong was full of question marks, but Lan Ruatong continued, "Let's go home. You've been freezing time for so long, you must be tired. Let my brother handle things here." What? What? Lon Shang Dome froze on the throne. His daughter, who had been cold and distant since childhood, suddenly became so considerate today? Was it just because he saved that boy she liked? Lan Shang Dong didn't understand, but he was deeply shaken. By the way, Lan Ruatong seemed to have thought of something. She turned her head, her eyes red as she smiled and said, "Thank you, Dad." And no, you're welcome. Lan Shang Dong felt his tongue tie up. Ever since his daughter entered adolescence, he hadn't seen her smile with a hint of coetishness like this. At this moment, Lan Shang Dong felt his heart completely healed. And he seemed to have realized something. He turned his gaze to Guu Yuan below, silently murmuring to himself, "I think I know how to win my daughter's favor now." Under the night sky, the cold wind howled. On the towering ice throne, Lon Shandong withdrew his scrutinizing gaze. He turned to Lan Yuding within the blockade and left a single sentence. The rest is up to you. Before his words had fully landed, he waved his hand and the space beneath the throne shattered like a mirror, instantly engulfing Lan Rouadong into the pitch black spatial rift. The swirling snow and ice vanished along with it, and the terrifying pressure weighing down on everyone disappeared without a trace. Amidst the ruins, Guuan looked at the slowly closing spatial rift in midair, a trace of doubt flashing through his mind. Lan Rouadong had been present from start to finish. Yet, she hadn't said a single word to him, not even exchanged a glance. Could it be because her father was nearby, and she didn't dare to act too obvious? Guan stroked his chin, feeling that this explanation made sense. In front of a strict father, it was normal for a girl to be a bit reserved. As he was pondering, the phone in his pocket suddenly vibrated. Guu Yuan took out his phone and a new message popped up on the screen. A message appeared sent by Lan Ruatong. The content consisted of just one word, hump. Guuan was momentarily stunned and replied, "What's wrong?" A few seconds later, another message came through from the other party. "Get some rest. Well talk tomorrow." Guu Yuan curled his lips. He could roughly guess why Lan Rouaton was upset. A few days ago, she had warned him not to come to the lower district, and he had agreed. Yet today, he caused such a commotion in the lower district that Luadong had to call her father for help. Now that the matter was resolved, it was only natural for her to start sulking. But it didn't matter. When the time came, he could just shift the blame onto Lon Rouadong's brother. He'd say it was her brother who insisted on using him as bait and that he couldn't refuse out of respect for Lan Ruatong. As long as you're fine," Lan Yuding waved dismissively, clearly unconcerned about the whereabouts of the corpse. "Then let's settle the payment." Guan immediately switched to a money-hungry demeanor. As agreed, 2 million for one werewolf. I handled the level 29 one by myself, so I get the full reward. As for the other two second tier werewolves, as per the agreement, I take 20% 40,000 for each commission. Lon Yuing was amused by him. Look at you so unambitious. He shot Guyu on a glance, pulled up a holographic screen, and quickly operated it. In this capture operation, you were the biggest contributor. The credit for the three werewolves is all yours, 6 million in total. The guild only takes a 5% handling fee. Guuan's eyes lit up. Her brother was truly generous. She had originally thought this private job would earn her at most 2.8 million, but it had doubled to 6 million. Even after deducting 5%, there was still 5.7 million left. For a newcomer, this was definitely a huge sum of money. Many veteran combat professionals, even after working for 10 years, might not save up this much. The money's settled. Now it's time to satisfy my curiosity. Lanuting closed the holographic screen, threw an arm around Guianuan's shoulder, and lowered his voice to ask, "What was that gray green vortex just now?" "I heard the captured werewolf say it was the trial of the god of wild hunt." "Yes, the wild hunt trial," Buuan answered truthfully. Holy crap. Luding couldn't help but curse. You really know how to stir up trouble, huh? Even a god got involved. What was this trial like? It was just hundreds or thousands of werewolves attacking me. The lowest level being 25 and quite a few at level 30, Guuan explained casually. Hundreds or thousands of level 25 to 30 werewolves? You call that a trial? Lan Yuding gasped, pressing for more details. And then, and then Guuan spread his hands. Then I held my ground. The trial ended, and I came out. Killed them all. Lan Yuding was completely stunned on the spot. He released his grip on Guu Yuan's shoulder and looked at the young man in front of him as if he were a monster. How did you manage to hold out? Luding couldn't comprehend it. Even for him, facing hundreds or thousands of level 30 werewolves alone would be dangerous. After all, stamina and mental strength aren't infinite. While he could wreak havoc, there would always come a moment of exhaustion. When he was so tired that he couldn't even perform basic attacks, he would still be overwhelmed and killed by the monsters. Guu Yuan was slightly agitated. He could tolerate people calling him useless, but he absolutely couldn't stand people saying he lacked skill. Using Night Phantom's Displacement to dodge attacks, redemption coffin to block damage, sacrifice gem to restore mana, sacrificing werewolves under the suppression of divine might, and even summoning Catherine at the most critical moment. Weren't these all examples of skillful operation? Even if most of the kills were made by summoned creatures, could you really say there was no skill involved? Moreover, I'm not barely over level 10. He took several deep breaths, forcing himself to calm down, but the shock in his eyes was impossible to hide. awakened for only half a month and already level 18.
